create database case_study;
use case_study;
CREATE TABLE OLYMPICS_HISTORY (
    id          INT,
    name        VARCHAR(100),
    sex         VARCHAR(100),
    age         VARCHAR(100),
    height      DECIMAL(5,2),
    weight      DECIMAL(5,2),
    team        VARCHAR(100),
    noc         VARCHAR(100),
    games       VARCHAR(100),
    year        VARCHAR(10),
    season      VARCHAR(100),
    city        VARCHAR(100),
    sport       VARCHAR(100),
    event       VARCHAR(100),
    medal       VARCHAR(100)
);

CREATE TABLE OLYMPICS_HISTORY_NOC_REGIONS (
    noc    VARCHAR(100),
    region VARCHAR(100),
    notes  VARCHAR(100)
);
